|ᎪᎦᏍᏗ|5|Talsgohi digokski degalo sagwu nidegakwenvsvi.|ᏔᏍᎵᏍᎪᎯ ᏗᎪᎦᏍᎩ ᏕᎦᎶ ᏌᏊ ᏂᏕᎦᏇᏅᏒᎢ.|There are twenty cigarettes in one package.|
|ᎨᎳᏗᏙᎭ|5|Tsgwisdi yvwi nunadvhnv uhweladidasdi ulvkwdi.|ᏥᏈᏍᏗ ᏴᏫ ᏄᎾᏛᎲ ᎤᏪᎳᏗᏓᏍᏗ ᎤᎸᏉᏗ.|He likes to mingle with a lot of people.|
|ᎦᏌᏆᎸᎢ|5|Gasagwalv gasgilo alsdayhdi unisgila junenvsvi.|ᎦᏌᏆᎸ ᎦᏍᎩᎶ ᎠᎵᏍᏓᏴᏗ ᎤᏂᏍᎩᎳ ᏧᏁᏅᏒᎢ.|They have a round dinner table at home.|
|ᏔᎷᎩᏍᎩ|5|Dahyasladisgo talugisgi yagohila ama yidalisdi.|ᏓᏯᏍᎳᏗᏍᎪ ᏔᎷᎩᏍᎩ ᏯᎪᎯᎳ ᎠᎹ ᏱᏓᎵᏍᏗ.|Cans get rusty if water is left in them too long.|
|ᏓᏆᎴᎳ|5|Digaduhv wigaluhjv asgaya, dagwalela dayuhwasi.|ᏗᎦᏚᎲ ᏫᎦᎷᏨ ᎠᏍᎦᏯ, ᏓᏆᎴᎳ ᏓᏳᏩᏏ.|When he gets to town, the man is going to buy a car.|
|ᎤᏕᎵᏍᎦᎸᎲᎢ|5|Eligwus yiksdela udelisgalvhv galesv dagwalela?|ᎡᎵᏊᏍ ᏱᏍᎩᏍᏕᎳ ᎤᏕᎵᏍᎦᎸᎲ ᎦᎴᏒ ᏓᏆᎴᎳ?|Can you help me get my car out of a ditch?|
|ᎦᏄᎪᎢᏍᏙᏗᎢ|5|Eligwus yiskinohis uhna gohlvsv ganugoisdohdii?|ᎡᎵᏊᏍ ᏱᏍᎩᏃᎯᏍ ᎤᎿ ᎪᏢᏒ ᎦᏄᎪᎢᏍᏙᏗᎢ?|Can you tell me where the exit is?|

|ᎠᏍᏆᎸᏂᎭ|5|Gosdvnisdi gvhdi usgwalvnisdi gihli unehltanvi.|ᎪᏍᏛᏂᏍᏗ ᎬᏗ ᎤᏍᏆᎸᏂᏍᏗ ᎩᏟ ᎤᏁᏟᏔᏅᎢ.|He tried to hit the dog on the head with a bat.|

|ᏗᎧᏃᏩᏛᏍᏗ|5|Dikanowadvsdi yiduniyostana igada gvwakti nanadvnehoi.|ᏗᎧᏃᏩᏛᏍᏗ ᏱᏚᏂᏲᏍᏔᎾ ᎢᎦᏓ ᎬᏩᎩᏘ ᎾᎾᏛᏁᎰᎢ.|When some people break the law, they get away with it.|

|ᎩᎦ ᏕᎧᏴᏍᏉᎢᎭ|5|Sgwahlesdi uwahnila kayvsoli giga duhyvsgwolvi.|ᏍᏆᏞᏍᏗ ᎤᏩᏂᎳ ᎧᏴᏐᎵ ᎩᎦ ᏚᏴᏍᏉᎸᎢ.|When a ball hit him on his nose, he got a nosebleed.|
|ᎠᎦᏓᎭᎢ|5|Gadohi yidunanelohna diniyohli, anigadaha nanalsdisgoi.|ᎦᏙᎯ ᏱᏚᎾᏁᎶᎿ ᏗᏂᏲᏟ, ᎠᏂᎦᏓᎭ ᎾᎾᎵᏍᏗᏍᎪᎢ.|When children play on the ground, they become dirty.|
|ᏕᎧᎵᏆᏕᎦ|5|Gajanuli uwadeystana adeyohv duhlihgwadinvsv dagwalela.|ᎦᏣᏄᎵ ᎤᏩᏕᏯᏍᏔᎾ ᎠᏕᏲᎲ ᏚᏟᏆᏗᏅᏒ ᏓᏆᎴᎳ.|When he went around the curve too fast, he turned the car over.|
|ᏓᏍᏔᏰᏍᎦ|5|Hlesdi vsgi isdayi yidijalvhwisdanehesdi, dotastayesis.|ᏞᏍᏗ ᎥᏍᎩ ᎢᏍᏓᏱ ᏱᏗᏣᎸᏫᏍᏓᏁᎮᏍᏗ, ᏙᏔᏍᏔᏰᏏᏍ.|Don't work so hard or you'll get exhausted.|
|ᎤᎵᏍᏆᎵᏓ|5|Gvnosasdi ulsgwalida jiyvwahta. Julsgwalida adiha.|ᎬᏃᏌᏍᏗ ᎤᎵᏍᏆᎵᏓ ᏥᏴᏩᏔ. ᏧᎵᏍᏆᎵᏓ ᎠᏗᎭ.|I found a broken broom. He says he's broke.|
|ᏚᎸᏫᏍᏓᏁᎭ|5|Na didehlohgwasgi Dodagwidena udodagwada dulvhwisdanehoi.|Ꮎ ᏗᏕᏠᏆᏍᎩ ᏙᏓᏈᏕᎾ ᎤᏙᏓᏆᏓ ᏚᎸᏫᏍᏓᏁᎰᎢ.|That student works all day Saturday.|
|ᏓᏓᏁᏎᎠ|5|Dadahnesesgv uwhtanidasdi uhyalv judahnesesdi ajitayosela.|ᏓᏓᏁᏎᏍᎬ ᎤᏮᏔᏂᏓᏍᏗ ᎤᏯᎸ ᏧᏓᏁᏎᏍᏗ ᎠᏥᏔᏲᏎᎳ.|He looked for his conjuring material when he was asked to conjure.|
|ᎦᎨᏓ|5|Nigohilv gageda asaladanvhvsgv nidigalsdohdi jinuhlinigvga.|ᏂᎪᎯᎸ ᎦᎨᏓ ᎠᏌᎳᏓᏅᎲᏍᎬ ᏂᏗᎦᎵᏍᏙᏗ ᏥᏄᏟᏂᎬᎦ.|The reason he is so strong is because he is always lifting heavy objects.|
|ᏕᎪᏏᏏᎭ|5|Unadodagwasgv Dinadehlohgwasgi digehyohvsgi duwosisahnv unigoliyevɂi.|ᎤᎾᏙᏓᏆᏍᎬ ᏗᎾᏕᏠᏆᏍᎩ ᏗᎨᏲᎲᏍᎩ ᏚᏬᏏᏌᏅ ᎤᏂᎪᎵᏰᎥᎢ.|The Sunday School teacher explained what they had read.|
|ᎦᏚᎲᎢ|6|Hila nania yvwi aneha Daligwa gaduhvi?|ᎯᎳ ᎾᏂᎠ ᏴᏫ ᎠᏁᎭ ᏓᎵᏆ ᎦᏚᎲᎢ?|What's the population of the town of Tahlequah?|
|ᏓᏁᎶᏗᎭ|6|Gada usdi danehldi na usdi achuja?|ᎦᏙ ᎤᏍᏗ ᏓᏁᎶᏗ Ꮎ ᎤᏍᏗ ᎠᏧᏣ?|What is the little boy playing with?|
|ᏎᎷ|6|Hila iga selu dehatvhisda kohi gogi|ᎯᎳ ᎢᎦ ᏎᎷ ᏕᎭᏛᎯᏍᏓ ᎪᎯ ᎪᎩ|How much corn did you raise this summer?|
|ᎤᏕᎦ|6|Sunale udli wijadesv na uyo gahldvi.|ᏑᎾᎴ ᎤᏟ ᏫᏣᏕᏒ Ꮎ ᎤᏲ ᎦᎵᏛᎢ.|Tomorrow throw the trash away.|
|ᎠᎦᏍᎦ|6|Tsgwisdi agasga dlv envsdi kohi iga.|ᏥᏈᏍᏗ ᎠᎦᏍᎦ Ꮲ ᎡᏅᏍᏗ ᎪᎯ ᎢᎦ.|It's raining too much to go somewhere today.|
|ᎦᎪ|6|Gago na sakonige ulsduli jigi asgaya?|ᎦᎪ Ꮎ ᏌᎪᏂᎨ ᎤᎵᏍᏚᎵ ᏥᎩ ᎠᏍᎦᏯ?|Who is the man wearing the blue cap?|
|ᎦᎵᏗᎭ|6|Gado usdi gahldi talugisgi na asgaya?|ᎦᏙ ᎤᏍᏗ ᎦᎵᏗ ᏔᎷᎩᏍᎩ Ꮎ ᎠᏍᎦᏯ?|What is the man putting in the can?|
|ᎦᏅᏅᎢ|6|Josgo joi gohweli ganvhnv nav jinela.|ᏦᏍᎪ ᏦᎢ ᎪᏪᎵ ᎦᏅᏅ ᎾᎥ ᏥᏁᎳ.|I live near highway 33.|
|ᏙᏧᏩ|6|Tojuwha usdika sihnv na dlayhga gesvi.|ᏙᏧᏮᎠ ᎤᏍᏗᎧ ᏏᏅ Ꮎ ᏜᏴᎦ ᎨᏒᎢ.|The redbird is smaller than the bluejay.|
|ᎦᎴᎦ|6|Wesa ukehena gihli, wesa hlgvi ulvsvi.|ᏪᏌ ᎤᎨᎮᎾ ᎩᏟ, ᏪᏌ ᏡᎬᎢ ᎤᎸᏒᎢ.|When the dog chased the cat, the cat climbed a tree.|
|ᏭᏕᎵᎦ|6|Wudeligv ididla wudeligo iga ehi nvda.|ᏭᏕᎵᎦ ᎢᏗᏜ ᏭᏕᎵᎪ ᎢᎦ ᎡᎯ ᏅᏓ.|The sun goes out of sight in the west.|
|ᎠᎦᏴᎵ|6|Agayvli saloli juhyo gihli uwaka eduji.|ᎠᎦᏴᎵ ᏌᎶᎵ ᏧᏲ ᎩᏟ ᎤᏩᎧ ᎡᏚᏥ.|My uncle has an old squirrel dog.|
|ᏯᏙᏟ|6|Hyatohli sdudi ktov wigalohisdi juwenvsv yoga.|ᏯᏙᏟ ᏍᏚᏗ ᎬᏙᎥ ᏫᎦᎶᎯᏍᏗ ᏧᏪᏅᏒ ᏲᎦ.|You go through a narrow gate when you're going to his house.|
|ᎠᎯᏓ|6|Igada inada hla ahida yigi digowhtvhdi.|ᎢᎦᏓ ᎢᎾᏓ Ꮭ ᎠᎯᏓ ᏱᎩ ᏗᎪᏩᏛᏗ.|Some snakes are not easy to see.|
|ᏏᏅ|6|Ije dagwawela dajehla sihnv uweti gesvi.|ᎢᏤ ᏓᏆᏪᎳ ᏓᏤᏝ ᏏᏅ ᎤᏪᏘ ᎨᏒᎢ.|A new car is better than an old one.|
|ᎤᎦᎾᏩ|6|Udohiyu uganawa nigalsda kohi iga, doka?|ᎤᏙᎯᏳ ᎤᎦᎾᏩ ᏂᎦᎵᏍᏓ ᎪᎯ ᎢᎦ, ᏙᎧ?|It sure got warm today, didn't it?|
|ᏂᎦᎵᏍᏗᎭ|6|Udohiyu uganawa nigalsda kohi iga, doka?|ᎤᏙᎯᏳ ᎤᎦᎾᏩ ᏂᎦᎵᏍᏓ ᎪᎯ ᎢᎦ, ᏙᎧ?|It sure got warm today, didn't it?|
|ᎤᏍᎪᎵ|6|Hlgv uskoli wulohlv saloli gihli ukehena.|ᏡᎬ ᎤᏍᎪᎵ ᏭᎶᏢ ᏌᎶᎵ ᎩᏟ ᎤᎨᎮᎾ.|The squirrel climbed to the top of the tree when the dog chased it.|
|ᎣᏍᏓ|6|Hia hawiya osda agisdi. Osd gawoni.|ᎯᎠ ᎭᏫᏯ ᎣᏍᏓ ᎠᎩᏍᏗ. ᎣᏍᏓ ᎦᏬᏂ.|This meat is good to eat. He speaks well.|
|ᎠᎦᎷᎦ|6|Igada agaluga jusdi geso, igadahno jutana.|ᎢᎦᏓ ᎠᎦᎷᎦ ᏧᏍᏗ ᎨᏐ, ᎢᎦᏓᏃ ᏧᏔᎾ.|Some twisters are small and some are big.|
|ᏓᎦᏟᎭ|6|Suhliloda iga selu duktlvhv sogwili ugisdi|ᏚᏟᎶᏓ ᎢᎦ ᏎᎷ ᏚᎦᏢᎲ ᏐᏈᎵ ᎤᎩᏍᏗ.|He shelled a bushel of corn for the horse to eat.|
|ᎦᎵᏣᏗ|6|Gado usdi ada hvhdisgo gahljadi yijohlvhna?|ᎦᏙ ᎤᏍᏗ ᎠᏓ ᎲᏗᏍᎪ ᎦᎵᏣᏗ ᏱᏦᏢᎿ?|What kind of wood do you use when you make a bow?|
|ᏓᏬᎵ|6|Igada dawoli anosda digahyesdi igadahno anadahihi.|ᎢᎦᏓ ᏓᏬᎵ ᎠᏃᏍᏓ ᏗᎦᏰᏍᏗ ᎢᎦᏓᏃ ᎠᎾᏓᎯᎯ.|Some mushrooms are good to eat but others are poisonous.|
|ᏕᎦᎾᏗᏫᏍᎦ|6|Nvnohi deganadiwsgv ahwi jigov usv jigesvi.|ᏅᏃᎯ ᏕᎦᎾᏗᏫᏍᎬ ᏥᎪᎥ ᎠᏫ ᎤᏒ ᏥᎨᏒᎢ.|I saw a deer crossing a road last night.|
|ᎠᏔᎴᏒᎢ|6|Nvya junsdi gvhdi tikalija datalesv nvnohi.|ᏅᏯ ᏧᎾᏍᏗ ᎬᏗ ᏘᎧᎵᏣ ᏓᏔᎴᏒ ᏅᏃᎯ.|Fill the holes in the road with gravel.|
|ᎦᏁᏐᏯᏍᎦ|6|Sudetiyvsa jigesv kohi iga sdaya unesoysvi.|ᏚᏕᏘᏴᏌ ᏥᎨᏒ ᎪᎯ ᎢᎦ ᏍᏓᏯ ᎤᏁᏐᏯᏒᎢ.|One year ago today it hailed hard.|
|ᎠᏕᎲᏍᎦ|6|Hisgi iyuwahnilv jigesv kohi sunale udehnvi.|ᎯᏍᎩ ᎢᏳᏩᏂᎸ ᏥᎨᏒ ᎪᎯ ᏑᎾᎴ ᎤᏕᏅᎢ.|He was born at five o'clock this morning.|
|ᏎᏗ|6|Igada disehisdi sedi ada digohlvhtanv gesoi.|ᎢᎦᏓ ᏗᏎᎯᏍᏗ ᏎᏗ ᎠᏓ ᏗᎪᏢᏔᏅ ᎨᏐᎢ.|Some dressers are made of walnut.|
|ᎠᎿᏬᎠ|6|Ije gasaleni ajinvnelv asehnv hla yuhnawoei.|ᎢᏤ ᎦᏌᎴᏂ ᎠᏥᏅᏁᎸ ᎠᏎᏅ Ꮭ ᏳᎿᏬᎡᎢ.|He was given a new coat, but he didn't wear it.|
|ᎡᏝᏪᎢ|6|Ehlawe gesv yvwi gawonisgi gawonisgv igohida.|ᎡᏝᏪ ᎨᏒ ᏴᏫ ᎦᏬᏂᏍᎩ ᎦᏬᏂᏍᎬ ᎢᎪᎯᏓ.|The people were quiet while the speaker spoke.|
|ᎠᏓᏃᏰᎭ|6|Udahnoyehdi uduli asehnv hla adahnoyo yuwaya.|ᎤᏓᏃᏰᏗ ᎤᏚᎵ ᎠᏎᏅ Ꮭ ᎠᏓᏃᏲ ᏳᏩᏯ.|He wants to fan herself, but he has no fan.|
|ᎤᏂᏡᎬᎢ|6|Uhnihlgvigwu iga uhlinohiya na utana jihlgvi.|ᎤᏂᏡᎬᎢᏊ ᎢᎦ ᎤᏟᏃᎯᏯ Ꮎ ᎤᏔᎾ ᏥᏡᎬᎢ.|A stump is all that's left of the big tree.|
|ᎠᎾᏟᏅᏟ|6|Hia hisgi iyanii anichuja nigada anahlinvdli.|ᎯᎠ ᎯᏍᎩ ᎢᏯᏂᎢ ᎠᏂᏧᏣ ᏂᎦᏓ ᎠᎾᏟᏅᏟ.|These five boys are all brothers.|
|ᏗᎦᎳᏫᏍᏗᎢ, ᏧᏂᎳᏫᏍᏗᎢ|6|Hila iga degohlv junilawisdi Daligwa gaduhvi?|ᎯᎳ ᎢᎦ ᏕᎪᏢ ᏧᏂᎳᏫᏍᏗ ᏓᎵᏆ ᎦᏚᎲᎢ?|How many churches are there in the city of Tahlequah?|
|ᎠᏓᏍᏓᏴᎲᏍᎦ|6|Hla ase jadasdayhdi yigi, hlaheno yagigosiha.|Ꮭ ᎠᏎ ᏣᏓᏍᏓᏴᏗ ᏱᎩ, ᏝᎮᏃ ᏯᎩᎪᏏᎭ.|You don't have to cook, because I'm not hungry.|
|ᎠᎪᏩᏛᏗ|6|Ije ganulvsv dohiyu uwoduhi agowhtvhdi gesoi.|ᎢᏤ ᎦᏄᎸᏒ ᏙᎯᏳ ᎤᏬᏚᎯ ᎠᎪᏩᏛᏗ ᎨᏐᎢ.|The green grass is really a beautiful sight.|
|ᎤᎸᏌᏗ|6|Sudali iga ama judlisdohdi julvsadi duhwasvi.|ᏑᏓᎵ ᎢᎦ ᎠᎹ ᏧᏟᏍᏙᏗ ᏧᎸᏌᏗ ᏚᏩᏒᎢ.|He bought six water glasses.|
|ᎦᏬᏂᎭ|6|Tsgwisdi gawoniha, asehnv hla gohusdi yadiha.|ᏥᏈᏍᏗ ᎦᏬᏂᎭ, ᎠᏎᏅ Ꮭ ᎪᎱᏍᏗ ᏯᏗᎭ.|He's talking a lot, but he's not saying anything.|
|ᏕᎬᏙᎯᎠ|6|Tuyunsdi degvtohia. Hila iga sohi dotvtohisi?|ᏚᏳᎾᏍᏗ ᏕᎬᏙᎯᎠ. ᎯᎳ ᎢᎦ ᏐᎯ ᏙᏛᏙᎯᏏ?|He's shelling peas. How many hickory nuts are you going to shell?|
|ᏫᎦᏅᎥᏍᎦ|6|Adela jutayosela uweji talsgo adelv wunvnelvi.|ᎠᏕᎳ ᏧᏔᏲᏎᎳ ᎤᏪᏥ ᏔᎵᏍᎪ ᎠᏕᎸ ᏭᏅᏁᎸᎢ.|When his son asked him for some money, he sent him a twenty dollar bill.|
|ᎭᏫᏂ|6|Eligwu tali iyatahwostanv yigeda amayi hawini.|ᎡᎵᏊ ᏔᎵ ᎢᏯᏔᏬᏍᏔᏅ ᏱᎨᏓ ᎠᎹᏱ ᎭᏫᏂ.|I can stay under water for two minutes.|
|ᎤᏁᎦ|6|Gigvha nulstanv unega uhnuwv giga duhyvsgwola.|ᎩᎬᎭ ᏄᎵᏍᏔᏅ ᎤᏁᎦ ᎤᏄᏮ ᎩᎦ ᏚᏴᏍᏉᎳ.|His white shirt got bloody when his nose started bleeding.|
|ᎠᏓᏨᎢᏍᎩ|6|gohusd usdi tsgoya adajvysgi uwajvhyv uwoyeni.|ᎪᎱᏍᏓ ᎤᏍᏗ ᏥᎪᏯ ᎠᏓᏨᎢᏍᎩ ᎤᏩᏨᏴ ᎤᏬᏰᏂ.|Some kind of a stinging bug stung him on his hand.|
|ᎤᏢᎩ|6|Hila iyanii junidlvgi aniyaa ahani junidlvgii?|ᎯᎳ ᎢᏯᏂᎢ ᏧᏂᏢᎩ ᎠᏂᏯᎠ ᎠᎭᏂ ᏧᏂᏢᎩᎢ?|How many patients are in this hospital?|
|ᎤᎵᏏᎩ|6|Sdayi agowhtvhdi ulsihgv kilo ulsihgi yuhnuwa.|ᏍᏓᏱ ᎠᎪᏩᏛᏗ ᎤᎵᏏᎬ ᎩᎶ ᎤᎵᏏᎩ ᏳᏄᏩ.|It's hard to see someone in the dark if he has on a dark shirt.|
|ᎠᎾᏓᏟᏏᎭ|6|Tsgwisdi yvwi anadahlisiha digaduhvi kohi iga.|ᏥᏈᏍᏗ ᏴᏫ ᎠᎾᏓᏟᏏᎭ ᏗᎦᏚᎲᎢ ᎪᎯ ᎢᎦ.|A lot of people are gathering in town today.|
|ᏧᎦᎾᏮᎢ|6|Juganawv didla danukdisgo sasa gola yinulstana.|ᏧᎦᏅᏮ ᏗᏜ ᏓᏄᎪᏗᏍᎪ ᏌᏌ ᎪᎳ ᏱᏄᎵᏍᏔᎾ.|Geese head south when winter comes.|
|ᎤᏒᏙᏂ|6|Ama juwedasdi jusvdoni dunesdaladv usv jigesvi.|ᎠᎹ ᏧᏪᏓᏍᏗ ᏧᏒᏙᏂ ᏚᏁᏍᏓᎳᏛ ᎤᏒ ᏥᎨᏒᎢ.|The water pipes froze last night.|
|ᏚᏠᏍᎦ|6|Hla kilo yulvkwdi uyo adanhdadisdi judlohisdii.|Ꮭ ᎩᎶ ᎤᎸᏉᏗ ᎤᏲ ᎠᏓᏅᏓᏗᏍᏗ ᏧᏠᎯᏍᏗᎢ.|No one likes to be confronted with a bad feeling.|
|ᎤᏁᏝᏅᎯ, ᎤᏁᏝᏅᎯ|6|Yihowa dudoa Unehlanvhi adiha Galvkwdi Gohweli.|ᏱᎰᏩ ᏚᏙᎠ ᎤᏁᏝᏅᎯ ᎠᏗᎭ ᎦᎸᏉᏗ ᎪᏪᎵ.|The Bible says God's name is Jehovah.|
|ᎦᏚ ᎤᎦᎾᏍᏓ|6|Gadu uganasda uwaduhnv uweji achuja udetiyisgvi.|ᎦᏚ ᎤᎦᎾᏍᏓ ᎤᏩᏚᏅ ᎤᏪᏥ ᎠᏧᏣ ᏚᏕᏘᏱᏍᎬᎢ.|He baked a cake for his son's birthday.|

|ᏑᏓᎵ|6|Sudali iyuwahnilv sunale didla uyeisdosgoi waji.|ᏑᏓᎵ ᎢᏳᏩᏂᎸ ᏑᎾᎴ ᏗᏜ ᎤᏰᎢᏍᏙᏍᎪᎢ ᏩᏥ.|The alarm clock wakes him up at six o'clock in the morning.|
|ᎠᏓᏩᏛᎯᏙᎭ|6|Hla ayv agwenvsv yigi ahani. Gadawahtvhidohagwu.|Ꮭ ᎠᏴ ᎠᏇᏅᏒ ᏱᎩ ᎠᎭᏂ. ᎦᏓᏩᏛᎯᏙᎭᏊ.|This isn't my home. I'm just visiting.|
|ᏥᏍᏆ|6|Igada jisgwa juganowv wanilosgo gola yinulstana.|ᎢᎦᏓ ᏥᏍᏆ ᏧᎦᏃᏮ ᏩᏂᎶᏍᎪ ᎪᎳ ᏱᏄᎵᏍᏔᎾ.|Some birds migrate south in the winter.|
|ᎦᏰᎪᎩ|6|Kilo gayhgogi yigi, julotsgi ganhdada anadisgoi.|ᎩᎶ ᎦᏴᎪᎩ ᏱᎩ, ᏣᎶᏥᎩ ᎦᏅᏓᏓ ᎠᎾᏗᏍᎪᎢ.|If someone is a liar, they say he has a forked tongue.|
|ᎠᏁᏍᎨᎭ|6|Na dihnesgesgi utana jitaga uniyvsdi uhnesgehvi.|Ꮎ ᏗᏁᏍᎨᏍᎩ ᎤᏔᎾ ᏥᏔᎦ ᎤᏂᏴᏍᏗ ᎤᏁᏍᎨᎲᎢ.|The carpenter built a big chicken house.|
|ᎦᏂᏱᎭ|6|Na gihli hiniya. Hilayv jigesv ajiniyvhe?|Ꮎ ᎩᏟ ᎯᏂᏯ. ᎯᎳᏴ ᏥᎨᏒ ᎠᏥᏂᏴᎮ?|Catch the dog. When was he arrested?|
|ᎠᏞᏤᎭ|6|Udlechehdi udulvhv asesgini hla vsgi yinudvnelei.|ᎤᏞᏤᏗ ᎤᏚᎸᎲ ᎠᏎᏍᎩᏂ Ꮭ ᎥᏍᎩ ᏱᏄᏛᏁᎴᎢ.|He wanted to take revenge against him but he didn't do it.|
|ᎦᏥᏃᏏᎭ|6|Ama ulohisdi usvdoni utsgwidvnelv asehnv uwachinosahnvi.|ᎠᎹ ᎤᎶᎯᏍᏗ ᎤᏒᏙᏂ ᎤᏥᏈᏛᏁᎸ ᎠᏎᏅ ᎤᏩᏥᏃᏌᏅᎢ.|The water pipe bent, but he straightened it out.|
|ᎤᏩᏥᏍᎦᏢᎢ|6|Gado usdi hvhdisgo hnvnhdesgv ajadi uwajisgahlvi?|ᎦᏙ ᎤᏍᏗ ᎲᏗᏍᎪ ᏅᏅᏕᏍᎩ ᎠᏣᏗ ᎤᏩᏥᏍᎦᏢᎢ?|What do you use to take fish scales off?|
|ᎦᎵᏦᎯᏓ|6|Na galijohida asgaya anehldi udagesv uyohusehdii.|Ꮎ ᎦᎵᏦᎯᏓ ᎠᏍᎦᏯ ᎠᏁᎵᏗ ᎤᏓᎨᏒ ᎤᏲᎱᏎᏗᎢ.|The fat man is trying to lose weight.|
|ᎢᎸᏍᎩ|6|Ilvsgi iyuhliloda eladi uhnigisvi kila udajanelvi.|ᎢᎸᏍᎩ ᎢᏳᏟᎶᏓ ᎡᎳᏗ ᎤᏂᎩᏒᎢ ᎩᎳ ᎤᏓᏣᏁᎸᎢ.|He walked a few miles before he caught a ride.|
|ᎦᏬᏅᏗᎭ|6|Unegujv iyusdi uweji achuja nigohilv gawonhdisgoi.|ᎤᏁᎫᏨ ᎢᏳᏍᏗ ᎤᏪᏥ ᎠᏧᏣ ᏂᎪᎯᎸ ᎦᏬᏅᏗᏍᎪᎢ.|Because his son is so mean, he always lectures him.|
|ᏜᏱᎦ|6|Dlayhgv, Ogalahomi, gaduhv jigi dlayhga dudostanei.|ᏜᏱᎬ, ᎣᎦᎳᎰᎻ, ᎦᏚᎲ ᏥᎩ ᏜᏱᎦ ᏚᏙᏍᏔᏁᎢ.|The town of Jay, Oklahoma, was named after the bluejay.|
|ᏚᎵᏍᏗ|6|Dulisdi kalv Anijalagi Daligwa unisgwalveho Unadetiyisgvi.|ᏚᎵᏍᏗ ᎧᎸ ᎠᏂᏣᎳᎩ ᏓᎵᏆ ᎤᏂᏍᏆᎸᎡᎰ ᎤᎾᏕᏘᏱᏍᎬᎢ.|Cherokee Holiday is held at Tahlequah in the month of September.|
|ᏣᎳᎩ, ᎠᏣᎳᎩ|6|Hila nania Anijalagi dunilvhwisdane Jalagi Ayehlii?|ᎯᎳ ᎾᏂᎠ ᎠᏂᏣᎳᎩ ᏚᏂᎸᏫᏍᏓᏁ ᏣᎳᎩ ᎠᏰᎵᎢ?|How many Cherokees work at the Cherokee Nation?|
|ᏓᏍᏓᏲᎯᎭ|6|Segajv dusdayohlv galogwe asdayv gojanesdii iyusdi.|ᏎᎦᏨ ᏚᏍᏓᏲᏢ ᎦᎶᏇ ᎠᏍᏓᏴ ᎪᏣᏁᏍᏗᎢ ᎢᏳᏍᏗ.|He barely shot the gun because the trigger was hard to pull.|
|ᎦᏌᏆᎴᎯᎭ|6|Nuhlinigvgv kdisgo yuwasagwalehla na utana gagwatdi.|ᏄᏟᏂᎬᎬ ᎬᏗᏍᎪ ᏳᏩᏌᏆᎴᏝ Ꮎ ᎤᏔᎾ ᎦᏆᏘᏗ.|He uses all his strength when he rolls the big wheel.|
|ᎦᏅᏍᎨᏂ|6|Ganvsgeni ajiyole dahnawoi ale aginvsdesdi nulstanei.|ᎦᏅᏍᎨᏂ ᎤᏩᏌᏙᏴ ᏍᏆᏞᏍᏗ.|He was shot in his leg in a war, and it had to be amputated.|
|ᎠᏗᏏᏯᎠ|6|Hidisiya gasgilo. Hla yudlanvda galadisdi dagwalelui.|ᎯᏗᏏᏯ ᎦᏍᎩᎶ. Ꮭ ᏳᏜᏅᏓ ᎦᎳᏗᏍᏗ ᏓᏆᎴᎷᎢ.|Leave the chair. There isn't room to put it in the car.|
|ᎠᏗᎦᎴᏯᎠ|6|Digohwel gasgilv duhlav dudigaleyv digohwelod uhyala.|ᏗᎪᏪᎵ ᎦᏍᎩᎸ ᏚᏝᎥ ᏚᏗᎦᎴᏴ ᏗᎪᏪᎶᏓ ᎤᏯᎳ.|He scattered the papers on the table when he looked for his pencil.|
|ᏧᎬᏩᎶᏗ|6|Galvladi jugvwahldi igesesdi hla yidvkiwasi dagwalela|ᎦᎸᎳᏗ ᏧᎬᏩᎶᏗ ᎢᎨᏎᏍᏗ, Ꮭ ᏱᏛᎩᏩᏏ ᏓᏆᎴᎳ|If the price is too high, I'm not going to buy the car.|
|ᏅᎩᏁᎢ|6|Kuyegwona nvhgine toi anedoho igada junilvhwisdanehi.|ᎫᏰᏉᎾ ᏅᎩᏁ ᏙᎢ ᎠᏁᏙᎰ ᎢᎦᏓ ᏧᏂᎸᏫᏍᏓᏁᎯ.|Some workers have a day off on the fourth of July.|
|ᎠᎵᏔᏬᎠ|6|Nigohilv ahltawosgo, vsgihnv iyusdi uwoduhi justihga.|ᏂᎪᎯᎸ ᎠᎵᏔᏬᏍᎪ, ᎥᏍᎩᏅ ᎢᏳᏍᏗ ᎤᏬᏚᎯ ᏧᏍᏘᎦ.|He combs his hair all the time, and that's why he has pretty hair.|
|ᎠᏰᎭ|6|Sgohi adelv jugvwahldi sagwu iyanadanhtehdi dahyehvi.|ᏍᎪᎯ ᎠᏕᎸ ᏧᎬᏩᏟᏗ ᏌᏊ ᎢᏯᎾᏓᏅᏖᏗ ᏓᏰᎲᎢ.|He had ten dollars worth of pennies in his hand.|
|ᏩᎲᏍᎦ|6|Vsgihyi talsgo nvhgine wuhnv Danisdayohihv adahnehdi.|ᎥᏍᎩᏱ ᏔᎵᏍᎪ ᏅᎩᏁ ᏭᏅ ᏓᏂᏍᏓᏲᎯᎲ ᎠᏓᏁᏗ.|He sent the Christmas gift on December the 24th.|
|ᏗᎦᎶᎩᏍᎩ|6|Digalogisgi uhwisvnv ukayosohnv nagasgvna gesv iyusdi.|ᏗᎦᎶᎩᏍᎩ ᎤᏫᏒᏅ ᎤᎧᏲᏐᏅ ᎾᎦᏍᎬᎾ ᎨᏒ ᎢᏳᏍᏗ.|The farmer's crop became dry because of no rain.|
|ᎦᏌᎾᎵ|6|Gasanali dayulenvhv adawelagisgv na gahljode jugohnvi.|ᎦᏌᎾᎵ ᏓᏳᎴᏅᎲ ᎠᏓᏪᎳᎩᏍᎬ Ꮎ ᎦᎵᏦᏕ ᏧᎪᏅᎢ.|The fire started at the roof when the house burned.|
|ᏑᎾᎴᎢ, ᏏᎾᎴᎢ|6|Sunale tali yuwahnilv jigesesdi dasvsdi digadlohisdii.|ᏑᎾᎴ ᏔᎵ ᏳᏩᏂᎸ ᏥᎨᏎᏍᏗ ᏓᏒᏍᏗ ᏗᎦᏠᎯᏍᏗᎢ.|Our meeting is scheduled for tomorrow at two o'clock.|
|ᎦᏣᎵᎪᏍᎦ|6|Gahljode uyvsdi yuduli wesa, galohisdi degajaligosgoi.|ᎦᎵᏦᏕ ᎤᏴᏍᏗ ᏳᏚᎵ ᏪᏌ, ᎦᎶᎯᏍᏗ ᏕᎦᏣᎵᎪᏍᎪᎢ.|When the cat wants to go inside the house, he scratches on the door.|
|ᏧᎿᏦᏍᏗ|6|Gohidi udihlehgv yigane unvdi juhnajosdi nigalsdisgoi.|ᎪᎯᏗ ᎤᏗᏞᎬ ᏱᎦᏁ ᎤᏅᏗ, ᏧᎿᏦᏍᏗ ᏂᎦᎵᏍᏗᏍᎪᎢ.|If milk is left out in the heat too long, it becomes sour.|
|ᎠᎵᏣᏙᎲᏍᎩ|6|Joi iyanii juweji anichuja anahljadohvsgi nunalstanvi.|ᏦᎢ ᎢᏯᏂᎢ ᏧᏪᏥ ᎠᏂᏧᏣ ᎠᎾᎵᏣᏙᎲᏍᎩ ᏄᎾᎵᏍᏔᏅᎢ.|Three of his sons became preachers.|
|ᎤᏪᏴᎢ|6|Aginulvhnv digisohisdi uweyvi sdayi ganohugisgv iyusdi.|ᎠᎩᏄᎸᏅ ᏗᎩᏐᎯᏍᏗ ᎤᏪᏴᎢ ᏍᏓᏱ ᎦᏃᎱᎩᏍᎬ ᎢᏳᏍᏗ.|I couldn't cross the river because it was too swift.|
|ᎦᎴᎠ|6|Ayehli ulesv udlawadvi. Dihnawo dulesv talujohi.|ᎠᏰᏟ ᎤᎴᏒ ᎤᏜᏩᏛᎢ. ᏗᎿᏬ ᏚᎴᏒ ᏔᎷᏦᎯ.|He took a half dollar out of his pocket. He took some clothes out of a basket|
|ᎦᏪᏐᎸᏍᏗᎭ|6|Ina yiduhilena wahga ilvsgi iyuwakdi degawesolvsdisgoi.|ᎢᎾ ᏱᏚᎯᎴᎾ ᏩᎦ ᎢᎸᏍᎩ ᎢᏳᏩᎦᏗ ᏕᎦᏪᏐᎸᏍᏗᏍᎪᎢ.|When he drives the cattle for a long distance he rests them a few times.|
|ᎤᏪᏥ ᎠᎨᏯ|6|Na udaji uwejihnv agehya unihloyi digegaganhdii.|Ꮎ ᎤᏓᏥ ᎤᏪᏥᏅ ᎠᎨᏯ ᎤᏂᏠᏱ ᏗᎨᎦᎦᏅᏗᎢ.|The mother and xher daughter look alike.|
|ᏑᏟᎶᏓ|6|Tali iyuhliloda uhilidolv suhliloda kanugahli gadesgvi.|ᏔᎵ ᎢᏳᏟᎶᏓ ᎤᎯᎵᏙᎸ ᏑᏟᎶᏓ ᎧᏄᎦᏟ ᎦᏕᏍᎬᎢ.|It took him two hours to pick a gallon of blackberries.|
|ᎠᏍᏆᏂᎪᏍᎦ|6|Usgwanigosv nahidiyv udehlohgwav ugoliyedi uweji achuja.|ᎤᏍᏆᏂᎪᏒ ᎾᎯᏗᏴ ᎤᏕᏠᏆᎥ ᎤᎪᎵᏰᏗ ᎤᏪᏥ ᎠᏧᏣ.|He was amazed at how fast his son learned to read.|
|ᎠᎳᏍᏓᎡᎭ|6|Alasdaesgv uhlv inada. Nigohilv yvwi dalasdaesgoi.|ᎠᎳᏍᏓᎡᏍᎬ ᎤᏢ ᎢᎾᏓ. ᏂᎪᎯᎸ ᏴᏫ ᏓᎳᏍᏓᎡᏍᎪᎢ.|He killed the snake by tromping on it. He always speaks badly of people.|
|ᏥᏆᎴᏆᎳ|6|Tsgwalegwala nigawesgv gatvgisgo julsihnvda adanelv navi.|ᏥᏆᎴᏆᎳ ᏂᎦᏪᏍᎬ ᎦᏛᎩᏍᎪ ᏧᎵᏏᏅᏓ ᎠᏓᏁᎸ ᎾᎥᎢ.|I hear a whippoorwill every night close to the house.|
|ᎠᏟᏴᏈᏛᏍᎦ|6|Dagwalela gvhdi uwahnila talugisgi getv, uhliyvhgwidvnvi.|ᏓᏆᎴᎳ ᎬᏗ ᎤᏩᏂᎳ ᏔᎷᎩᏍᎩ ᎨᏛ, ᎤᏟᏴᏈᏛᏅᎢ.|When he hit the steel post with a car, it bent.|
|ᏗᎫᎪᏗᏍᎩ|6|Josgo jusvhida junadasdudi uyvsdi duwukdanelv digukdisgi.|ᏦᏍᎪ ᏧᏒᎯᏓ ᏧᎾᏓᏍᏚᏗ ᎤᏴᏍᏗ ᏚᏬᎪᏓᏁᎸ ᏗᎫᎪᏗᏍᎩ.|The judge sentenced him to thirty days in jail.|
|ᏗᎾᏓᏅᏟ|6|Dinadahnvhlis hia anichuja? Kohiyv dagaluhji dinadahnvhli.|ᏗᎾᏓᏅᏟᏍ ᎯᎠ ᎠᏂᏧᏣ? ᎪᎯᏴ ᏓᎦᎷᏥ ᏗᎾᏓᏅᏟ.|Are these boys brothers? His brother is coming in a little while.|
|ᎠᏓᏁᏗ|6|Danisdayohihv nav yigi, didahnehdi anadaneanesvhvsgo yvwi.|ᏓᏂᏍᏓᏲᎯᎲ ᎾᎥ ᏱᎩ, ᏗᏓᏁᏗ ᎠᎾᏓᏁᎠᏁᏒᎲᏍᎪ ᏴᏫ.|When it's close to Christmas, people shop for gifts.|
|ᎠᎬᏓᎨᏂ|6|Ganiyisgi sgwahlesdi ganiyisgv dunvda agvdageni uwahnilvi.|ᎦᏂᏱᏍᎩ ᏍᏆᏞᏍᏗ ᎦᏂᏱᏍᎬ ᏚᏅᏓ ᎠᎬᏓᎨᏂ ᎤᏩᏂᎸᎢ.|When the catcher missed catching the ball, it hit him on his forehead.|
|ᎦᏌᏙᏍᎦ|6|Suhliloda iyudanvhida uwasadohyv dagwalela kila uhnigisvi.|ᏑᏟᎶᏓ ᎢᏳᏓᏅᎯᏓ ᎤᏩᏌᏙᏴ ᏓᏆᎴᎳ ᎩᎳ ᎤᏂᎩᏒᎢ.|He pushed the car for a mile before it started.|
|ᎦᎶᏁᎠ|6|Dodajiloneisv gayewsgi asehnv gayula juloneda gesvi.|ᏙᏓᏥᎶᏁᎢᏒ ᎦᏰᏫᏍᎩ ᎠᏎᏅ ᎦᏳᎳ ᏧᎶᏁᏓ ᎦᏒᎢ.|I was going to oil the sewing machine, but he had already oiled it.|
|ᎦᏐᏆᏘ|6|Gachinosda nalsdvhlusgvna gesv iyusdi gasohgwati nulstanvi.|ᎦᏥᏃᏍᏓ ᎾᎵᏍᏛᏡᏍᎬᎾ ᎨᏒ ᎢᏳᏍᏗ ᎦᏐᏆᏘ ᏄᎵᏍᏔᏅᎢ.|He became humpbacked because he wouldn't sit up straight.|
|ᎦᎷᏯᏍᏗ|6|Judanvgalvda nidowahnvna yigi dijesdo galuysdi yanhkilvvga.|ᏧᏓᏅᎦᎸᏓ ᏂᏙᏩᏅᎾ ᏱᎩ ᏗᏤᏍᏙ ᎦᎷᏯᏍᏗ ᏯᎾᎩᎸᎥᎦ.|If you don't keep the mattresses clean, bed bugs will get on them.|
|ᎠᏍᏚᎲᏍᎦ|6|Hisduhvga galohisdii. Uhyvsdeda yigi kilo asduhvsgoi.|ᎯᏍᏚᎲᎦ ᎦᎶᎯᏍᏗᎢ. ᎤᏴᏍᏕᏓ ᏱᎩ ᎩᎶ ᎠᏍᏚᎲᏍᎪᎢ.|Close the door. If someone is drunk, he jails him.|
|ᏓᎦᏘᏅᏛᏍᎦ|6|Igada agalisgv yanedoha julsihgi diktinvtdi danaktinvtvsgoi.|ᎢᎦᏓ ᎠᎦᎵᏍᎬ ᏯᏁᏙᎭ ᏧᎵᏏᎩ ᏗᎦᏘᏅᏘᏗ ᏓᎾᎦᏘᏅᏛᏍᎪᎢ.|When some people are in the sun, they put on dark glasses.|
|ᎠᏓᎾᏁᏒᎲᏍᎦ|6|Tsgwisdi udananesvhvsdi uduli asehnv tsgwisdi dagvwahldidana.|ᏥᏈᏍᏗ ᎤᏓᎾᏁᏒᎲᏍᏗ ᎤᏚᎵ ᎠᏎᏅ ᏥᏈᏍᏗ ᏓᎬᏩᎶᏗᏓᎾ.|He wants to do a lot of shopping, but the prices are too high.|
|ᏂᎬᎢ|6|Nikv uwehisdanelidoha adiha. Nikv uwedolidasdi ulvkwdi.|ᏂᎬ ᎤᏪᎯᏍᏓᏁᎵᏙᎭ ᎠᏗᎭ. ᏂᎬ ᎤᏪᏙᎵᏓᏍᏗ ᎤᎸᏉᏗ.|He says he hurts all over. He likes to go everywhere.|
|ᏍᏊ, ᎥᏍᏊ|6|Kohi iga dagilvhwisdaneha, sunalehnv vsgwu dodvgilvhwisdaneli.|ᎪᎯ ᎢᎦ ᏓᎩᎸᏫᏍᏓᏁᎭ, ᏑᎾᎴᏅ ᎥᏍᏊ ᏙᏛᎩᎸᏫᏍᏓᏁᎵ.|I am working today, and I will work tomorrow also.|
|ᎤᎦᎶᎦ|6|Uligohvsdi iyv jugaloga judalehnvda julisuhwida nidodagalstani.|ᎤᎵᎪᎲᏍᏗ ᎢᏴ ᏧᎦᎶᎦ ᏧᏓᎴᏅᏓ ᏧᎵᏑᏫᏓ ᏂᏙᏓᎦᎵᏍᏔᏂ.|In the fall the leaves will turn into different colors.|
|ᏓᏒᏍᏗᎭ|6|Unadodagwohnv usv uwonihisdi dusvstanvi gvwhtayosela uwonihisdii.|ᎤᎾᏙᏓᏉᏅ ᎤᏒ ᎤᏬᏂᎯᏍᏗ ᏚᏒᏍᏔᏅᎢ ᎬᏩᏔᏲᏎᎳ ᎤᏬᏂᎯᏍᏗᎢ.|He scheduled his speech for Monday night when asked to speak.|
|ᎠᏲᏟ|6|Diniyohli sgwahlesdi dananelohvsga. Diyohli nvya duwutesvi.|ᏗᏂᏲᏟ ᏍᏆᎴᏍᏗ ᏓᎾᏁᎶᎲᏍᎦ. ᏗᏲᏟ ᏅᏯ ᏚᏭᏖᏒᎢ.|The children are playing ball. He picked up some small rocks.|
|ᏗᏣᎳᎩ|6|Nigadu iyagwadetiyvda jigesv agwadehlohgwav Dijalagi digigoliyedii.|ᏂᎦᏚ ᎢᏯᏆᏕᏘᏴᏓ ᏥᎨᏒ ᎠᏆᏕᏠᏆᎥ ᏗᏣᎳᎩ ᏗᎩᎪᎵᏰᏗᎢ.|I learned to read Cherokee when I was fourteen years old.|
|ᎠᎱᏣᏬᎳᏛᎢ|6|Sdikidagwu aksgani didla yudijakahnana, yuhwigohwahta ahujawoladvi.|ᏍᏗᎩᏓᏊ ᎠᎦᏍᎦᎾᎢ ᏗᏜ ᏳᏗᏣᎧᎿᎾ, ᏳᏫᎪᏩᏔ ᎠᎱᏣᏬᎳᏛᎢ.|If you will look just a little to the left, you will see a chimney.|
|ᏃᏯ, ᏃᏱ|6|Degalanvdv yidunesdalada noya anilageydvsgoi nvnohi junilvhwisdanehi.|ᏕᎦᎳᏅᏛ ᏱᏚᏁᏍᏓᎳᏓ ᏃᏯ ᎠᏂᎳᎨᏯᏛᏍᎪᎢ ᏅᏃᎯ ᏧᏂᎸᏫᏍᏓᏁᎯ.|When the streets freeze over, the road maintenance crews dump sand on them.|
|ᎠᏓᏱᎭ|6|Unosgisv aguistana, udahyilvi. Jiyadayiha, hlahehno yijiyoliga.|ᎤᏃᏍᎩᏒ ᎠᎫᎢᏍᏔᎾ, ᎤᏓᏱᎸᎢ. ᏥᏯᏓᏱᎭ, ᏝᎮᏃ ᏱᏥᏲᎵᎦ.|When he was accused of stealing, he denied it. I am denying him because I don't know him.|
|ᎪᎢ|6|Unigodi Anijalagi dinadehlohgwasgi danadehlogwasgo Goi Junadehlohgwasdi.|ᎤᏂᎪᏗ ᎠᏂᏣᎳᎩ ᏗᎾᏕᏠᏆᏍᎩ ᏓᎾᏕᏠᏆᏍᎪ ᎪᎢ ᏧᎾᏕᏠᏆᏍᏗ.|A lot of Cherokee students go to school at Greasy School.|
|ᎠᏴᏈᏛᏍᎦ|6|Hlesdi jihihyvhgwidvni! Jisgwadv jiyewisgv hyehgahli dajiyvhgwidvni.|ᏞᏍᏗ ᏥᎯᏴᏈᏛᏂ! ᏥᏍᏆᏛ ᏥᏰᏫᏍᎬ ᏰᎦᏟ ᏓᏥᏴᏈᏛᏂ.|Don't bend it! When I finish sewing the quilt, I am going to hem it.|
|ᎪᎱᏍᏗ, ᎪᏍᏗ|7|Gohusdi unihyo asehnv hla yagwanhta iyusdi gesvi.|ᎪᎱᏍᏗ ᎤᏂᏲ ᎠᏎᏅ Ꮭ ᏯᏆᎾᏔ ᎢᏳᏍᏗ ᎨᏒᎢ.|They are looking for something, but I don't know what it is.|
|ᎢᏤᎢ|7|Uweti dagwalela juhv asehnv nogwu ije uha.|ᎤᏪᏘ ᏓᏆᎴᎳ ᏧᎲ ᎠᏎᏅ ᏃᏊ ᎢᏤ ᎤᎭ.|He used to have an old car, but now he has a new one.|
|ᎠᎦᎵᎭ|7|Usgosdi agalisgo nvda iyuhno kali nvda yigi.|ᎤᏍᎪᏍᏗ ᎠᎦᎵᏍᎪ ᏅᏓ ᎢᏳᏃ ᎧᎵ ᏅᏓ ᏱᎩ.|The moon shines brightly if it's a full moon.|
|ᎠᎵᏖᎸᎲᏍᎦ|7|Hla ulihwojv yigi na inada. Si ahltelvhvsgagwu.|Ꮭ ᎤᎵᏬᏨ ᏱᎩ Ꮎ ᎢᎾᏓ. Ꮟ ᎠᎵᏖᎸᎲᏍᎦᏊ.|The snake isn't dead. It's still moving.|
|ᎦᏍᏉᎢᎭ|7|Ama gasgwoiha na gadulida ahnawo jigada asildvi.|ᎠᎹ ᎦᏍᏆᎣᎢᎭ Ꮎ ᎦᏚᎵᏓ ᎠᎿᏬ ᏥᎦᏓ ᎠᏏᎳᏛᎢ.|Water is dripping from the wet cloth hanging on a line.|
|ᎤᎧᏲᏓ|7|Nelagi jugahnanv svhi, gayula ukahyoda igi gadohi.|ᏁᎳᎩ ᏧᎦᎿᏅ ᏒᎯ, ᎦᏳᎳ ᎤᎧᏲᏓ ᎢᎩ ᎦᏙᎯ.|Although it rained yesterday, the ground is already dry.|
|ᎦᏅᏃᏩ|7|Selu uda gohlvhtanv ganvnowa goksdisgi gesvi edudu.|ᏎᎷ ᎤᏓ ᎪᏢᏔᏅ ᎦᏅᏃᏩ ᎪᎦᏍᏗᏍᎩ ᎨᏒᎢ ᎡᏚᏚ.|My grandfather used to smoke a corncob pipe.|
|ᎤᏍᏗ|7|Jusdi dagwalela ugodi dagilvgwdi sihnv jutana gesvi.|ᏧᏍᏗ ᏓᏆᎴᎳ ᎤᎪᏗ ᏓᎩᎸᏉᏗ ᏏᏅ ᏧᏔᎾ ᎨᏒᎢ.|I like small cars better than big ones.|
|ᏅᏲᎯ|7|Nvyohi Odalv dudov ganela. Nvyohi uwohlvhnv dlogesi.|ᏅᏲᎯ ᎣᏓᎸ ᏚᏙᎥ ᎦᏁᎳ. ᏅᏲᎯ ᎤᏬᏢᏅ ᏠᎨᏏ.|He lives in a place called Rocky Mountain. He made a garden in a rocky place.|
|ᎤᎫᎫ|7|Igada udalehi anelisgo uguku yinigawea adanelv navi.|ᎢᎦᏓ ᎤᏓᎴᎯ ᎠᏁᎵᏍᎪ ᎤᎫᎫ ᏱᏂᎦᏪᎠ ᎠᏓᏁᎸ ᎾᎥᎢ.|Some people think it is a bad omen to hear a hoot owl close to a building.|
|Ꮭ ᎢᎸᎯᏳ|7|Igada yvwi hla ilvhiyu junadasdudi uniyvhlv yigesoi.|ᎢᎦᏓ ᏴᏫ Ꮭ ᎢᎸᎯᏳ ᏧᎾᏓᏍᏚᏗ ᏱᎨᏐᎢ.|Some people have never been in jail.|
|ᏗᏓᏰᏠᎯ|7|Na usdi achuja didahyehlohi iyulsdohdi uduli atvsvi.|Ꮎ ᎤᏍᏗ ᎠᏧᏣ ᏗᏓᏰᏠᎯ ᎢᏳᎵᏍᏙᏗ ᎤᏚᎵ ᎠᏛᏒᎢ.|That little boy wants to become a surgeon when he grows up.|
|ᏅᏯ|7|Digagedi gesv disaladodi nvya kilo nosdelisgvna yigi.|ᏗᎦᎨᏗ ᎨᏒ ᏗᏌᎳᏙᏗ ᏅᏯ ᎩᎶ ᏃᏍᏕᎵᏍᎬᎾ ᏱᎩ.|The rocks were too heavy to lift if no one helped.|
|ᎫᏖᎠ|7|Gayula kilo jinvwistana juwutesdi hia nvya janilageya.|ᎦᏳᎳ ᎩᎶ ᏥᏅᏫᏍᏔᎾ ᏧᏭᏖᏍᏗ ᎯᎠ ᏅᏯ ᏔᏂᎳᎨᏯ.|I've already asked someone to pick these rocks up.|
|ᎤᏬᏝ|7|1. Hadlv iyv johlesdi? 2. Uwohlas disdadahnvhli?|1. ᎭᏢ ᎢᏴ ᏦᏞᏍᏗ? 2. ᎤᏬᏝᏍ ᏗᏍᏓᏓᏅᏟ?|1. Where will you be sitting? 2. Is your brother home?|
|ᎧᏬᎳᏕᎠ|7|Na achuja udanvhida udanawstanv iyusdi sdaya kawoladea.|Ꮎ ᎠᏧᏣ ᎤᏓᏅᎯᏓ ᎤᏓᎾᏩᏍᏔᏅ ᎢᏳᏍᏗ ᏍᏓᏯ ᎧᏬᎳᏕᎠ.|The boy is breathing hard because he ran a long distance.|
|ᎢᎦᏘ|7|Sudal ilasihdi, sudal isihtadisdi igati na alasgalisgi.|ᏑᏓᎵ ᎢᎳᏏᏗ, ᏑᏓᎵ ᎢᏏᏔᏗᏍᏗ ᎢᎦᏘ Ꮎ ᎠᎳᏍᎦᎵᏍᎩ.|That ballplayer is six feet, six inches tall.|
|ᎠᏓᏬᏍᏗᎢ|7|Uweyv agwadawosdi ugodi agilvkwdi sihnv adawosdi gesvi.|ᎤᏪᏴ ᎠᏆᏓᏬᏍᏗ ᎤᎪᏗ ᎠᎩᎸᏉᏗ ᏏᏅ ᎠᏓᏬᏍᏗ ᎨᏒᎢ.|I like to swim in a creek more than in a swimming pool.|
|ᎪᏍᏓᏱ|7|Ajila utsgati gvhdi akdlvha galuysdi, gosdayi nulstanvi.|ᎠᏥᎳ ᎤᏥᎦᏘ ᎬᏗ ᎠᎩᏢᎦᎭ ᎦᎷᏯᏍᏗ ᎪᏍᏓᏱ ᏄᎵᏍᏔᏅᎢ.|When I sharpened the axe with a file, it became sharp.|
|ᎠᎦᏍᎦᏂ|7|Aktisi didla wudlesv anisoihno aksgani didla wunadlesvi.|ᎠᎦᏘᏏ ᏗᏜ ᏭᏞᏒ ᎠᏂᏐᎢᏃ ᎠᎦᏍᎦᏂ ᏗᏜ ᏭᎾᏞᏒᎢ.|He turned right but the others turned left.|
|ᎤᏓᎴᎯ|7|Koga nigawesgv yatvgana usv, udalehi anadisgo Anijalagi.|ᎪᎦ ᏂᎦᏪᏍᎬ ᏯᏛᎦᎾ ᎤᏒ, ᎤᏓᎴᎯ ᎠᎾᏗᏍᎪ ᎠᏂᏣᎳᎩ.|Cherokees say that if you hear a crow at night, it's a bad omen.|
|ᎠᎵᎬᏓᏃᏍᏙᏗ|7|Na ganvhida ustihgi jigi Ayvwiya aligvdanosdohdi uduliha.|Ꮎ ᎦᏅᎯᏓ ᎤᏍᏘᎩ ᏥᎩ ᎠᏴᏫᏯ ᎠᎵᎬᏓᏃᏍᏙᏗ ᎤᏚᎵᎭ.|The Indian with the long hair wants a headband.|
|ᎠᏒᎲᏍᎦ|7|Suhliloda goi usvhnvi. Ulvsadi kali unvdi usvhnvi.|ᏑᏟᎶᏓ ᎪᎢ ᎤᏒᏅᎢ. ᎤᎸᏌᏗ ᎧᎵ ᎤᏅᏗ ᎤᏒᏅᎢ.|It used up one gallon of oil. He drank up a glass full of milk.|
|ᎤᏲᏨᎢ|7|Ulvsadi uyojv gutea. Udohiyu uyojv ayohli uwekaha.|ᎤᎸᏌᏗ ᎤᏲᏨ ᎫᏖᎠ. ᎤᏙᎯᏳ ᎤᏲᏨ ᎠᏲᏟ ᎤᏪᎧᎭ.|He's picking up a broken glass. He has a very spoiled child.|
|ᏆᏄᎾᏍᏗᎢ|7|Gogi yinulstana kwanunsdii degadesgo eji ale degahldisgoi.|ᎪᎩ ᏱᏄᎵᏍᏔᎾ ᏆᏄᎾᏍᏗᎢ ᏕᎦᏕᏍᎪ ᎡᏥ ᎠᎴ ᏕᎦᎶᏗᏍᎪᎢ.|Every summer my mother picks plums and cans them.|
|ᎠᎩᏏ|7|Sgohi iyanii jitaga anigisi dejigowhtiha, sagwuhnv achvya.|ᏍᎪᎯ ᎢᏯᏂᎢ ᏥᏔᎦ ᎠᏂᎩᏏ ᏕᏥᎪᏩᏘᎭ, ᏌᏊᏅ ᎠᏨᏯ.|I see ten hens and one rooster.|
|ᎠᏓᏅᎠ|7|Sgohi judetiyvda uneladvi Daligwa, kila uduluhv udanvsdii.|ᏍᎪᎯ ᏧᏕᏘᏴᏓ ᎤᏁᎳᏛᎢ ᏓᎵᏆ, ᎩᎳ ᎤᏚᎷᎲ ᎤᏓᏅᏍᏗᎢ.|He lived in Tahlequah for ten years, the he wanted to move.|
|ᎠᏑᏴᏍᎦ|7|Svgi inage ehi yunvhnistana Anijalagi, juweji dansuyvsgoi.|ᏒᎩ ᎢᎾᎨ ᎡᎯ ᏳᏅᏂᏍᏔᎾ ᎠᏂᏣᎳᎩ, ᏧᏪᏥ ᏓᎾᏑᏴᏍᎪᎢ.|When Cherokees cook wild onions, they mix them with eggs.|
|ᎣᎦᎳᎰᎹ|7|Ogalahoma jigi "gigage asgaya" adiha Anijahda uniwonihisdi.|ᎣᎦᎳᎰᎹ ᏥᎩ "ᎩᎦᎨ ᎠᏍᎦᏯ" ᎠᏗᎭ ᎠᏂᏣᏓ ᎤᏂᏬᏂᎯᏍᏗ.|Oklahoma means "red man" in the Choctaw language.|
|ᎦᏗᎨᏂ|7|Gadigeni uhyehlalv gugu uyojv ulasdvtana amayi aduhinidohvi.|ᎦᏗᎨᏂ ᎤᏰᏝᎸ ᎫᎫ ᎤᏲᏨ ᎤᎳᏍᏛᏔᎾ ᎠᎹᏱ ᎠᏚᎯᏂᏙᎲᎢ.|A broken glass cut his heel when he stepped on it while wading in water.|
|ᎠᏂᎩᏍᏗᎭ|7|Dagwalela uhnigisdohdi uduli, asehnv hla disduisdi yiduwaya.|ᏓᏆᎴᎳ ᎤᏂᎩᏍᏙᏗ ᎤᏚᎵ, ᎠᏎᏅ Ꮭ ᏗᏍᏚᎢᏍᏗ ᏱᏚᏩᏯ.|He wants to start the car but he doesn't have the keys.|
|ᎦᏅᏗᎠ|7|Dlv sgohi iyuwakdi nidusasehnv asehnv dunvdisilov agonisgvi.|Ꮲ ᏍᎪᎢ ᎢᏳᏩᎦᏗ ᏂᏚᏌᏎᏅ ᎠᏎᏅ ᏚᏅᏗᏍᎢᎶᎥ ᎠᎪᏂᏍᎬᎢ.|He fired about ten times, but he missed the target over and over.|
|ᎦᏓ|7|Gadaha elohi ideha; hadlvgwu yuwigiluhja gada idigowhtisgoi.|ᎦᏓᎭ ᎡᎶᎯ ᎢᏕᎭ; ᎭᏢᏊ ᏳᏫᎩᎷᏣ ᎦᏓ ᎢᏗᎪᏩᏘᏍᎪi.|We all live in a dirty world; no matter where we go we see dirt.|
|ᏗᏕᏠᏆᏍᎩ|7|Sohnel sgohi iyanii dinadehlohgwasgi dunisgwadv kohi gogeyi.|ᏐᏁᎳᏍᎪᎯ ᎢᏯᏂᎢ ᏗᎾᏕᏠᏆᏍᎩ ᏚᏂᏍᏆᏛ ᎪᎯ ᎪᎨᏱ.|Ninety students graduated this spring.|
|ᎠᏑᎴᎠ|7|Asiladv adawohiladisgv uyostana usulo usulesv osda nuwanelvi.|ᎠᏏᎳᏛ ᎠᏓᏬᎯᎳᏗᏍᎬ ᎤᏲᏍᏔᎾ ᎤᏑᎶ ᎤᏑᎴᏒ ᎣᏍᏓ ᏄᏩᏁᎸᎢ.|When he tore his pants while crossing over a fence, he took them off and mended them.|
|ᎢᏯᎦᏴᎵ|7|Joi iyagayvli iyani yvwi unatvdastanihlv ugvwiyuhi gawonisgvi.|ᏦᎢ ᎢᏯᎦᏴᎵ ᎢᏯᏂ ᏴᏫ ᎤᎾᏛᏓᏍᏔᏂᏢ ᎤᎬᏫᏳᎯ ᎦᏬᏂᏍᎬᎢ.|Three thousand people came to hear the President speak.|
|ᎠᏙᎩᏯᏍᎩ|7|Na asgaya jigawoni Amayehli ugvwiyuhi yigalsdisgi atohgiyasgi.|Ꮎ ᎠᏍᎦᏯ ᏥᎦᏬᏂ ᎠᎹᏰᏟ ᎤᎬᏫᏳᎯ ᏱᎦᎵᏍᏗᏍᎩ ᎠᏙᎩᏯᏍᎩ.|The man making he speech is a candidate for president of the United States.|
|ᎤᎦᎾᏬᏍᎦ|7|Agiganawosgadv sdikida nogwu. Osi nav uwohla uganawosga.|ᎠᎩᎦᎾᏬᏍᎦᏛ ᏍᏗᎩᏓ ᏃᏊ. ᎣᏏ ᎾᎥ ᎤᏬᏝ ᎤᎦᎾᏬᏍᎦ.|I am getting warm a little now. He's sitting by the stove warming himself.|
|ᎧᏬᏂ|7|Kawohni taline, sohneladu isgohitsgwa nvksgo sudali agwadehnei.|ᎧᏬᏂ ᏔᎵᏁ, ᏐᏁᎳᏚ ᎢᏍᎪᎯᏥᏆ ᏅᎩᏍᎪ ᏑᏓᎵ ᎠᏆᏕhᏁᎢ.|I was born April second, nineteen hundred forty six.|
|ᎠᏟᎶᎠ|7|Dihnesgesgi ahlilosdi kdisgo ahlilosgv iyv usgwalsdii hyahtena.|ᏗᏁᏍᎨᏍᎩ ᎠᏟᎶᏍᏗ ᎬᏗᏍᎪ ᎠᏟᎶᏍᎬ ᎢᏴ ᎤᏍᏆᎵᏍᏗᎢ ᏯᏖᎾ.|A carpenter uses a ruler in measuring the place where he cuts the board.|
|ᎠᏤᏫᎠ|7|Gadohi ajewia ama. Tsgwisdi adela yiduha, dajewisgoigwu.|ᎦᏙᎯ ᎠᏤᏫᎠ ᎠᎹ. ᏥᏈᏍᏗ ᎠᏕᎳ ᏱᏚᎭ, ᏓᏤᏫᏍᎪᎢᏊ.|He's spilling water on the ground. When he' s got a lot of money, he just wastes it.|
|ᏓᏠᏱᎭ|7|Wasgwalahiyv udahlgv Galvkwdi Gohweli, "Jisa dudlohilvi," adiha.|ᏩᏍᏆᎳᎯᏴ ᎤᏓᏡᎬ ᎦᎸᏉᏗ ᎪᏪᎵ, "ᏥᏌ ᏚᏠᎯᎸᎢ," ᎠᏗᎭ.|The shortest verse in the bible says, "Jesus wept."|
|ᏱᏂᎦᎵᏍᏗᎭᏊ ᎢᎸᏢᎢ|7|Yinigalsdihagwu ilvhdlv uwenvsdi yuduli ego yinigalsdihagwu iyvi.|ᏱᏂᎦᎵᏍᏗᎭᏊ ᎢᎸᏢ ᎤᏪᏅᏍᏗ ᏳᏚᎵ ᎡᎪ ᏱᏂᎦᎵᏍᏗᎭᏊ ᎢᏴᎢ?|He goes wherever he wants to go anytime.|
|ᎢᏳᏓᎵ|7|Hila iyudali dehihwisgo selu? Hila iyudali chawahtvhidohoi?|ᎯᎳ ᎢᏳᏓᎵ ᏕᎯᏫᏍᎪ ᏎᎷ? ᎯᎳ ᎢᏳᏓᎵ ᏣᏩᏛᎯᏙᎰᎢ?|How far apart do you plant your corn? How often does he visit you?|
|ᎠᏟᎠᏙ|7|Juwoduhi didliado duniha Anijalagi Unohlvhnvnv Unadananvi Daligwa.|ᏧᏬᏚᎯ ᏗᏟᎠᏙ ᏚᏂᎭ ᎠᏂᏣᎳᎩ ᎤᏃᏢᏅᏅ ᎤᎾᏓᎾᏅᎢ ᏓᎵᏆ.|They have some pretty earrings at the Cherokee Arts and Crafts in Tahlequah.|
|ᎬᏜᏗᎭ|7|Hvhdlada gotvi; doyu udihlehga. Dajvstv duwhladv anagalisgi.|ᎲᏜᏓ ᎪᏛᎢ; ᏙᏳ ᎤᏗᏞᎦ. ᏓᏨᏍᏛ ᏚᏮᎳᏛ ᎠᎾᎦᎵᏍᎩ.|Put out the fire; it's too hot. The lightning put the lights out.|
|ᎤᎨᏳᎭ|7|Ugeyuha waji hlale kilo yvgvtolsda. Higeyusesdi tsdayvhvsgi.|ᎤᎨᏳᎭ ᏩᏥ ᏝᎴ ᎩᎶ ᏴᎬᏙᎵᏍᏓ. ᎯᎨᏳᏎᏍᏗ ᏣᏍᏓᏴᎲᏍᎩ.|He's stingy with his watch and won't loan it to anyone. Love your wife.|
|ᎬᏗ|7|Ganvgwalosdi gvhdi uwahnilv yvgi. Jalagi gvhdi duhlinohehhri.|ᎦᏅᏆᎶᏍᏗ ᎬᏗ ᎤᏩᏂᎸ ᏴᎩ. ᏣᎳᎩ ᎬᏗ ᏚᎵᏃᎮᏢᎢ|He hit the nail with a hammer. He conversed by means of Cherokee.|
|ᎦᏓᎷᎩᎠ|7|Gohigiyv jigese dinilogisgi sogwili danhdisge danidalugisgv dlogesi.|ᎪᎯᎩᏴ ᏥᎨᏎ ᏗᏂᎶᎩᏍᎩ ᏐᏈᎵ ᏓᏅᏗᏍᎨ ᏓᏂᏓᎷᎩᏍᎬ ᏠᎨᏏ.|Long ago the farmers used horses for plowing the fields.|
|ᎬᏂᎭ|7|Gosdvnihi sdayi uwahnilv sgwahlesdi. Kilo gvhniha galohisdii.|ᎪᏍᏛᏂᎯ ᏍᏓᏱ ᎤᏩᏂᎸ ᏍᏆᏞᏍᏗ. ᎩᎶ ᎬᏂᎭ ᎦᎶᎯᏍᏗᎢ.|The batter hit the ball hard. Someone is knocking at the door.|
|ᎧᏃᎯᏰᎩ|7|Joi iyanvda iyudali Kanohiyegi analsdayvhvsgo Anijalagi Dinadawosgi.|ᏦᎢ ᎢᏯᏅᏓ ᎢᏳᏓᎵ ᎧᏃᎯᏰᎩ ᎠᎾᎵᏍᏓᏴᎲᏍᎪ ᎠᏂᏣᎳᎩ ᏗᎾᏓᏬᏍᎩ.|Cherokee Baptists eat Passover Supper every three months.|
|ᏗᎦᎴᏅᎯᏓ|7|Digalenvhida gihli digalenvhida asiladv uwudalvchelv galeni ganvhisv.|ᏗᎦᎴᏅᎯᏓ ᎩᏟ ᏗᎦᎴᏅᎯᏓ ᎠᏏᎳᏛ ᎤᏭᏓᎸᏤᎸ ᎦᎴᏂ ᎦᏅᎯᏒ.|The long-eared hound dog got his ear caught in the fence because his ear was so long.|
|ᎢᏳᏟᎶᏓ|7|Joi iyuhliloda iyudanvhida uhwidvhv tali iyuhliloda kanugahli.|ᏦᎢ ᎢᏳᏟᎶᏓ ᎢᏳᏓᏅᎯᏓ ᎤᏫᏛᎲ ᏔᎵ ᎢᏳᏟᎶᏓ ᎧᏄᎦᏟ.|He carried two gallons of blackberries for three miles.|
|ᏍᎪᎯ|7|Sgohi iyuwahnilv nidulsihnisv gagatosdisgo kanoheda adayvlatvsgi agihvi.|ᏍᎪᎯ ᎢᏳᏩᏂᎸ ᏂᏚᎵᏏᏂᏒ ᎦᎦᏙᏍᏗᏍᎪ ᎧᏃᎮᏓ ᎠᏓᏴᎳᏛᏍᎩ ᎠᎩᎲᎢ.|I watch the news at ten o'clock each night on my television set.|
|ᏥᏈᏍᏗ|7|Tsgwisdi gawonisgo osda yudanhta. Tsgwisdi aniyonega gajigowhtiha.|ᏥᏈᏍᏗ ᎦᏬᏂᏍᎪ ᎣᏍᏓ ᏳᏓᏅᏔ. ᏥᏈᏍᏗ ᎠᏂᏲᏁᎦ ᎦᏥᎪᏮᏘᎭ.|He talks a lot when he feels well. I see many white men.|
|ᏗᏂᏓᎿᏫ|7|Gadohv dinidahnawi nunalstanei? Dinidahnawi jaisv wugoha, ulitisvi.|ᎦᏙᎲ ᏗᏂᏓᎿᏫ ᏄᎾᎵᏍᏔᏁᎢ? ᏗᏂᏓᎿᏫ ᏣᎢᏒ ᏭᎪᎭ, ᎤᎵᏘᏒᎢ.|Why did they become enemies? When he saw his enemy coming, he ran away.|
|ᎠᎵᏍᏇᏚᎲᏍᎦ|7|Digaduhv yuwena judanvgalvda dahnawosgoi osdahno alsgwetuwo alsgwetuhvsgoi.|ᏗᎦᏚᎲ ᏳᏪᎾ ᏧᏓᏅᎦᎸᏓ ᏓᎿᏬᏍᎪᎢ ᎣᏍᏓᏃ ᎠᎵᏍᏇᏚᏬ ᎠᎵᏍᏇᏚᎲᏍᎪᎢ.|When he goes to town, he puts on clean clothes and a good hat.|
|ᎠᎦᏔᎲᎠ|7|Kilo uhyanisgv utvgana uktahvsvi. Winuluhjvnagwu uktahvsdi udulvhvi.|ᎩᎶ ᎤᏯᏂᏍᎬ ᎤᏛᎦᎾ ᎤᎦᏔᎲᏒᎢ. ᏫᏄᎷᏨᎾᏊ ᎤᎦᏔᎲᏍᏗ ᎤᏚᎸᎲᎢ.|When he heard someone calling him, he turned around. He wanted to turn back before he got there.|
|ᎫᏓᎸᏍᎦ|7|Sogwili unadudalvdi uwudalvnv sogwili ujelii. Degudalvvgas anagalisgi?|ᏐᏈᎵ ᎤᎾᏚᏓᎸᏗ ᎤᏩᏓᎸᏅ ᏐᏈᎵ ᎤᏣᎵᎢ. ᏕᎫᏓᎸᎢᎦᏍ ᎠᎾᎦᎵᏍᎩ?|He hitched up his horse at the hitching post. Did he hook up the battery?|
|ᎠᏛᏅᎢᏍᏗᎭ|7|Dlv agwenvsdi gadvnvisdiha. Tsgwisdi alsdayhdi advnvisdisgo Danisdayohihvi.|Ꮲ ᎠᏇᏅᏍᏗ ᎦᏛᏅᎢᏍᏗᎭ. ᏥᏈᏍᏗ ᎠᎵᏍᏓᏴᏗ ᎠᏛᏅᎢᏍᏗᏍᎪ ᏓᏂᏍᏓᏲᎯᎲᎢ.|I'm getting ready to go somewhere. He prepares a lot of food at Christmas.|
|ᎤᏢᎦ|8|Svhi jigesv akdlvgv asehnv osigwu igi kohi iga.|ᏒᎯ ᏥᎨᏒ ᎠᎩᏢᎬ ᎠᏎᏅ ᎣᏏᏊ ᎢᎩ ᎪᎯ ᎢᎦ.|I was sick yesterday, but I'm all right today.|
|ᎦᏬᎠ|8|Chuhga yigvwala gihli gawosgoi. Sgohi iyanii yvwi duwovi.|ᏧᎦ ᏱᎬᏩᎳ ᎩᏟ ᎦᏬᏍᎪᎢ. ᏍᎪᎯ ᎢᏯᏂᎢ ᏴᏫ ᏚᏬᎥᎢ.|If the dog has fleas, he bathes it. He baptized ten people.|
|ᎦᏃᏴᎦ|8|1. Na jiyu ganoyvga. 2. Hila iyv ganoyvgesdi?|1. ᏥᏳ ᎦᏃᏴᎦ. 2. ᎯᎳ ᎢᏴ ᎦᏃᏴᎨᏍᏗ?|1. The boat is sinking. 2. When will he be buried?|
|ᎬᏅᎢ|8|Na asgaya yvwi uhlvi gvnvi igohida ajisdudi dudukdasi.|Ꮎ ᎠᏍᎦᏯ ᏴᏫ ᎤᏢᎢ ᎬᏅᎢ ᎢᎪᎯᏓ ᎠᏥᏍᏚᏗ ᏚᏚᎪᏓᏏ.|The murderer was sentenced to life imprisonment.|
|ᎤᎵᏍᏆᎷᏓ|8|Kilo jolani ulsgwaluda asehnv hla yagwanhta vsgi gesvi.|ᎩᎶ ᏦᎳᏂ ᎤᎵᏍᏆᎷᏓ ᎠᏎᏅ Ꮭ ᏯᏆᏅᏔ ᎥᏍᎩ ᎨᏒᎢ.|Someone is sticking his head out of the window, but I don't know who it is.|
|ᎪᎵᎦ|8|Vsgwu sgohi nadetiya gvwagohv yigi kilo, ahida gohlgoi.|ᎥᏍᏊ ᏍᎪᎯ ᎾᏕᏘᏯ ᎬᏩᎪᎲ ᏱᎩ ᎩᎶ, ᎠᎯᏓ ᎪᎵᎪᎢ.|Even if it's been ten years since he has seen someone, he recognizes him easily.|
|ᏫᎦᎧᎲᏍᎦ|8|Dlv yega, nav ijunadali diganelv wigakahvsgo uweji ayohli.|Ꮲ ᏰᎦ, ᎾᎥ ᎢᏧᎾᏓᎵ ᏗᎦᏁᎸ ᏫᎦᎧᎲᏍᎪᎢ ᎤᏪᏥ ᎠᏲᏟ.|Whenever he goes somewhere, he takes his child to his neighbor.|
|ᎩᎳ|8|Kila usv agihlvhnv usv jigesvi. Kila wijisduhvga jolani.|ᎩᎳ ᎤᏒ ᎠᎩᏢᏅ ᎤᏒ ᏥᎨᏒᎢ. ᎩᎳ ᏫᏥᏍᏚᎲᎦ ᏦᎳᏂ.|I went to sleep early last night. I have just closed the window.|
|ᎥᏍᎩᏅ ᎢᏳᏍᏗ|8|Tsgwisdi jugvwahldi gesv gahljode; vsgihnv iyusdi hla yakiwasei.|ᏥᏈᏍᏗ ᏧᎬᏩᎶᏗ ᎨᏒ ᎦᎵᏦᏕ; ᎥᏍᎩᏅ ᎢᏳᏍᏗ Ꮭ ᏯᎩᏩᏎᎢ.|The house cost too much; therefore I didn't buy it.|
|ᏥᎩᎵᎵ|8|Jigilili yinigawe adanelv nav, kilo dagaluhji anadisgo Anijalagi.|ᏥᎩᎵᎵ ᏱᏂᎦᏪ ᎠᏓᏁᎸ ᎾᎥ, ᎩᎶ ᏓᎦᎷᏥ ᎠᎾᏗᏍᎪ ᎠᏂᏣᎳᎩ.|When a chickadee sings near a house, Cherokees say that someone will come.|
|ᎢᎦᏅᎯᏓ|8|Hiksgo ilasihdi iganvhida sdeyida uwhtanv wahga agina asladisgvi.|ᎯᎩᏍᎪ ᎢᎳᏏᏗ ᎢᎦᏅᎯᏓ ᏍᏕᏱᏓ ᎤᏮᏔᏅ ᏩᎦ ᎠᎩᎾ ᎠᏍᎳᏗᏍᎬᎢ.|He used a rope fifty feet long in roping a calf.|
|ᎦᏕᎠ|8|Svkta uwansv ugisdi udesvi. Hadagi ahnawo asiladv jigadaa.|ᏒᎦᏔ ᎤᏩᏂᏒ ᎤᎩᏍᏗ ᎤᏕᏒᎢ. ᎭᏓᎩ ᎠᎿᏬ ᎠᏏᎳᏛ ᏥᎦᏓᎠ.|He picked a ripe apple to eat. Take the shirt down from the line.|
|ᎦᏓᎭᎢ|8|Hla yudulvhe gadaha dagwalela uhilvsdi, vsgihnv iyusdi unvgalvhvi.|Ꮭ ᏳᏚᎸᎮ ᎦᏓᎭ ᏓᏆᎴᎳ ᎤᎯᎸᏍᏗ, ᎥᏍᎩᏅ ᎢᏳᏍᏗ ᎤᏅᎦᎸᎲᎢ.|He didn't want to drive a dirty car, so he washed it.|
|ᎠᏓᏲᏁᎯ|8|Jani osda kanohedv chaneline ayatohlv ajineisdi adahyonehi agehya.|ᏣᏂ ᎣᏍᏓ ᎧᏃᎮᏛ ᏣᏁᎵᏁ ᎠᏯᏙᏢ ᎠᏥᏁᎢᏍᏗ ᎠᏓᏲᏁᎯ ᎠᎨᏯ.|An adulteress is mentioned in chapter eight of the book of John.|
|ᎦᎶᏍᎦ|8|Gosdi nudvhnvna ulosv ojidonav navi. Ahida ulosv ajigoliyea.|ᎪᏍᏗ ᏄᏛᏅᎾ ᎤᎶᏒ ᎣᏥᏙᎾᎥ ᎾᎥᎢ. ᎠᎯᏓ ᎤᎶᏒ ᎠᏥᎪᎵᏰᎠ.|He passed by them and me without even saying anything. He passed easily when he was tested.|
|ᎬᎾᏬᏍᎦ|8|Gvnawosgi gohlvhtanv ulvsadi uwanawosv udihlehg ama adlisdv wuhlana.|ᎬᎾᏬᏍᎩ ᎪᏢᏔᏅ ᎤᎸᏌᏗ ᎤᏩᎾᏬᏒ ᎤᏗᏞᎩ ᎠᎹ ᎠᏟᏍᏛ ᏭᏝᎾ.|A glass made of plastic melted when he put it in some hot water.|
|ᎠᏱᎭ|8|Hisgi dije digohwelodi duyvhv didananvi. Eladi waya digohwelodi.|ᎯᏍᎩ ᏗᏤ ᏗᎪᏪᎶᏗ ᏚᏴᎲ ᏗᏓᎾᏅᎢ. ᎡᎳᏗ ᏩᏯ ᏗᎪᏪᎶᏗ.|He got five new pencils from the store. He picked up a pencil from the ground.|
|ᎠᎬᎭᎵᎭ|8|Asano uwohlvhdi ugvhalvhvi. Hayelsdi gvhdi agvhali gadu uganasda.|ᎠᏌᏃ ᎤᏬᏢᏗ ᎤᎬᎭᎸᎲᎢ. ᎭᏰᎵᏍᏗ ᎬᏗ ᎠᎬᎭᎵ ᎦᏚ ᎤᎦᎾᏍᏓ.|He cut a pattern for a dress. He's slicing the cake with a knife.|
|ᎠᎵᏘᎠ|8|Jisdu jiniyvhvi svhi asehnv agwalitielvi. Junadasdudi ayav ulitisvi.|ᏥᏍᏚ ᏥᏂᏴᎲᎢ ᏒᎯ ᎠᏎᏅ ᎠᏆᎵᏘᎡᎸᎢ. ᏧᎾᏓᏍᏚᏗ ᎠᏯᎥ ᎤᎵᏘᏒᎢ.|I caught a rabbit yesterday, but it ran away from me. He escaped from jail.|
|ᏓᎾᏠᏍᎦ|8|Tsgwisdi Anijalagi dunadlosv Daligwa ugvwiyuhi gawonisgv unatvgodi uniyelvsvi.|ᏥᏈᏍᏗ ᎠᏂᏣᎳᎩ ᏚᎾᏠᏒ ᏓᎵᏆ ᎤᎬᏫᏴᎯ ᎦᏬᏂᏍᎬ ᎤᎾᏛᎪᏗ ᎤᏂᏰᎸᏒᎢ.|A lot of Cherokees met at Tahlequah in order to hear the chief speak.|
|ᎠᎪᎵᏰᎠ|8|Oginalii nidayunvnv gohwel jigoliyea. Aganakti ugoliyedi udulisgv udlvgi.|ᎣᎩᎾᎵᎢ ᏂᏓᏳᏅᏅ ᎪᏪᎵ ᏥᎪᎵᏰᎠ. ᎠᎦᎾᎦᏘ ᎤᎪᎵᏰᏗ ᎤᏚᎵᏍᎬ ᎤᏢᎩ.|I am reading a letter from a friend. The patient wanted a doctor to examine him.|
|ᎦᏌᏁᎾᏛᏍᎦ|8|Asti gasanenadvsga yvgii. Juksvsdi uwasanenadvnv uweti dagwalela udanawstana|ᎠᏍᏘ ᎦᏌᏁᎾᏛᏍᎦ ᏴᎩᎢ. ᏧᎦᏒᏍᏗ ᎤᏩᏌᏁᎾᏛᏅ ᎤᏪᏘ ᏓᏆᎴᎳ ᎤᏓᎾᏫᏍᏔᎾ.|He's threading a needle. The old car left a trail of smoke as it took off.|
|ᎧᏃᎮᏓ|8|Kanoheda kanohesgi kanoheda kanoheha. Ahljadohvsgi kanoheda duhljadohnelv yvwi.|ᎧᏃᎮᏓ ᎧᏃᎮᏍᎩ ᎧᏃᎮᏓ ᎧᏃᎮᎭ. ᎠᎵᏣᏙᎲᏍᎩ ᎧᏃᎮᏓ ᏚᎵᏣᏙᏁᎸ ᏴᏫ.|The newscaster is telling the news. A preacher preached the gospel to the people.|
|ᎨᏡᎲᏍᎦ|8|Wahya yidutvgana gihli gehluhvsgoi. Unaligosv unadahlosa, unehluhnv analasgalisgi.|ᏩᏯ ᏱᏚᏛᎦᎾ ᎩᏟ ᎨᏡᎲᏍᎪᎢ. ᎤᎾᎵᎪᏒ ᎤᎾᏓᏠᏌ, ᎤᏁᏡᏅ ᎠᎾᎳᏍᎦᎵᏍᎩ.|The dog howls when he hears the wolves. When their team won, the ballplayers yelled.|
|ᏎᏓᏂ|9|Sedani dijadlosv nigesvna yigi kohi iga, eligwu ijulaha yisdai.|ᏎᏓᏂ ᏗᏣᏠᏒ ᏂᎨᏒᎾ ᏱᎩ ᎪᎯ ᎢᎦ, ᎡᎵᏊ ᎢᏣᎳᎭ ᏱᏍᏓᎢ.|If you haven't been confronted by Satan today, it's possible you two are walking in the same direction.|
|ᎬᏕᎦ|9|Hila iyv jigesv uwhdeje anineli? Hla yagwanhte nehvna gesvi.|ᎯᎳ ᎢᏴ ᏥᎨᏒ ᎤᏮᏕᏤ ᎠᏂᏁᎵ? Ꮭ ᏯᏆᏅᏖ ᏁᎲᎾ ᎨᏒᎢ.|When did his husband part with him? I didn't know he was not living.|
|ᎠᏯᏂᎭ|9|Wahga uhyona gvhdi ahyaniha gihli. Hadlv hiyanvhe hia gihli?|ᏩᎦ ᎤᏲᎾ ᎬᏗ ᎠᏯᏂᎭ ᎩᏟ. ᎭᏢ ᎯᏯᏅᎮ ᎯᎠ ᎩᏟ?|He's calling the dog with a cow horn. Where did you get this dog?|
|ᎠᎦᎳᏍᎦ|9|Na agehyuja ustihgv ugalsdi uduli. Juwoyeni gvhdi ugalsv asti.|Ꮎ ᎠᎨᏳᏣ ᎤᏍᏘᎬ ᎤᎦᎳᏍᏗ ᎤᏚᎵ. ᏧᏬᏰᏂ ᎬᏗ ᎤᎦᎳᏒ ᎠᏍᏘ.|The girl wants to cut xher hair. He broke the string with his hands.|
|ᏏᏊ|9|Svhi aktvganv sigwu digawonisisv kohi iga. Sigwu agwaduli ama.|ᏒᎯ ᎠᏆᏛᎦᏅ ᏏᏊ ᏗᎦᏬᏂᏏᏒ ᎪᎯ ᎢᎦ. ᏏᏊ ᎠᏆᏚᎵ ᎠᎹ.|I heard yesterday that he was supposed to speak again today. I want more water.|
|ᎤᏍᎦᏃᎵ|9|Igada unisganoli geso unadvnvisdohdii. Usganoli galohi nigvwsdi kohi iga.|ᎢᎦᏓ ᎤᏂᏍᎦᏃᎵ ᎨᏐ ᎤᎾᏛᏅᎢᏍᏙᏗᎢ. ᎤᏍᎦᏃᎵ ᎦᎶᎯ ᏂᎬᏩᏍᏗ ᎪᎯ ᎢᎦ.|Some people are slow to get ready. Today seemed to go by slow.|
|ᎠᏯᏙᎯᎯ|9|Galohni talsgo hisgine, sohneladu isgohitsgwa gahlgwasgo joi ayatohihi nulstanvi.|ᎦᎶᏂ ᏔᎵᏍᎪ ᎯᏍᎩᏁ, ᏐᏁᎳᏚ ᎢᏍᎪᎯᏥᏆ ᎦᏟᏆᏍᎪ ᏦᎢ ᎠᏯᏙᎯᎯ ᏄᎵᏍᏔᏅᎢ.|He became a deacon on August 25, 1973.|
|ᏓᏓᎿᏫᏍᏗᎭ|9|Dudov uwohwelodi asdanvhnv dudahnawstanvi naktahvna gesv iyusdi Gilisi uwohwelodii.|ᏚᏙᎥ ᎤᏬᏪᎶᏗ ᎠᏍᏓᏅᏅ ᏚᏓᎿᏫᏍᏔᏅᎢ ᎾᎦᏔᎲᎾ ᎨᏒ ᎢᏳᏍᏗ ᎩᎵᏏ ᎤᏬᏪᎶᏗᎢ.|He made an X on the signature line because he didn't know how to write his name in English.|
|ᎤᏴᏜ|9|Ajalagi uhyvdla "yuniyvha" hla uhyvdla yiganiyisgoi, uhyvdlasgini ugvwisyuso uniyisgoi.|ᎠᏣᎳᎩ ᎤᏴᏜ "ᏳᏂᏴᎭ" Ꮭ ᎤᏴᏜ ᏱᎦᏂᏱᏍᎪᎢ, ᎤᏴᏜᏍᎩᏂ ᎤᎬᏫᏍᏳᏐ ᎤᏂᏱᏍᎪᎢ.|Whenever a Cherokee "catches" a cold, he doesn't catch the cold; rather, the cold catches him.|
|ᏅᏓ|10|Iga ehi nvda ugodi utana sihnv svnoyi ehi nvda gesvi.|ᎢᎦ ᎡᎯ ᏅᏓ ᎤᎪᏗ ᎤᏔᎾ ᏏᏅ ᏒᏃᏱ ᎡᎯ ᏅᏓ ᎨᏒᎢ.|The sun is bigger than the moon.|
|ᎤᎵᏍᏓᏁᎭ|10|Gosdi ulsdahnelv dlv wedohv. Hla yiuluhjei. Gado ulsdahne na gihli?|ᎪᏍᏗ ᎤᎵᏍᏓᏁᎸ Ꮲ ᏪᏙᎲ. Ꮭ ᏱᎤᎷᏤᎢ. ᎦᏙ ᎤᎵᏍᏓᏁ Ꮎ ᎩᏟ?|Something happened to him while he was away. He didn't come back. What's wrong with that dog?|
|ᎦᏙ ᎤᏍᏗ|10|Gado usdi higowhtiha? Ijeiyusdi digohwelodi. Gado usdi jaduliha? ksdehldi agwaduli.|ᎦᏙ ᎤᏍᏗ ᎯᎪᏩᏘᎭ? ᎢᏤ ᎢᏳᏍᏗ ᏗᎪᏪᎶᏗ. ᎦᏙ ᎤᏍᏗ ᏣᏚᎵᎭ? ᏍᎩᏍᏕᎸᏗ ᎠᏆᏚᎵ.|What do you see? A green pencil. What do you want? I want you to help me.|
